msg:During the 5.1 period in Zhuji, I first booked a double bed in a top-ranked hotel while navigating on a certain Debit card. Unexpectedly, the hotel said "cannot confirm" and refunded my order. I went to check the room again and found that it was +100 yuan again... speechless. Decisively quit these immature and shameless suppliers.
Enter Ctrip and continue to look for a double bed room. The information here is much more reliable, but the top rankings are also the ones that have raised the room price. Without saying much, I continue to scroll down and see Xiangsheng. Xiangsheng also has a place in Putuo Mountain. I have stayed there and it feels good. Click in and find the target room. It actually has everything, only 450 yuan. I can take my baby to take a bath, swim, and eat an almost five-star breakfast. Wow, it really surprised me. It is more than two levels higher than the hotel that squeezed in six or seven hundred to eat on the street beach two days ago.
Xiangsheng is the hotel I am most satisfied with since the holiday travel after the epidemic. It is luxurious, high-quality, honest and trustworthy. I highly recommend it and thank Ctrip for providing this high-quality option.
